href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-dev">tb dev</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-endpoint">tb endpoint</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-fmt">tb fmt</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-info">tb info</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-init">tb init</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-infra">tb infra</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-job">tb job</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-local">tb local</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 pipe</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" aria-hidden="true" class="overflow-hidden transition-all" style="max-height:0"><div class="pt-2" style="padding-inline-start:16px"><ul class="space-y-2 border-l border-v-border"><li><a class="block class="text-sm font-semibold">Compliance</h5></a></li></ul></div><div class="border-y border-v-border mt-4 md:mt-auto md:border-b-0 py-2 px-2"><a class="py-2 px-3 flex gap-x-2 items-center rounded cursor-pointer w-full outline-none t-body-3-semibold hover:bg-v-bg-active focus:bg-v-bg-active" href="/docs/changelog"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill="currentColor" d="M2.473 10.86a.7.7 0 0 0-.22-.14.67.67 0 0 0-.507 0 .7.7 0 0 0-.22.14.7.7 0 0 0-.14.22.67.67 0 0 0 .14.727q.099.089.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .22-.14.67.67 0 0 0 .14-.727.7.7 0 0 0-.14-.22m2.194-5.527H14A.667.667 0 1 0 14 4H4.667a.667.667 0 0 0 0 1.333M2.473 7.527a.67.67 0 0 0-.726-.14.8.8 0 0 0-.22.14.7.7 0 0 0-.14.22.63.63 0 0 0 0 .506q.05.123.14.22.097.09.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .506 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .22-.14.8.8 0 0 0 .14-.22.63.63 0 0 0 0-.506.7.7 0 0 0-.14-.22M14 7.333H4.667a.667.667 0 0 0 0 1.334H14a.667.667 0 1 0 0-1.334M2.473 4.193a.7.7 0 0 0-.22-.14.67.67 0 0 0-.727.14.8.8 0 0 0-.14.22.63.63 0 0 0 0 .507q.052.121.14.22.099.089.22.14a.67.67 0 0 0 .727-.14.8.8 0 0 0 .14-.22.63.63 0 0 0 0-.507.8.8 0 0 0-.14-.22M14 10.667H4.667a.667.667 0 1 0 0 1.333H14a.666.666 0 1 0 0-1.333"></path></svg>Changelog</a></div><div class="relative md:hidden inset-0 top-auto"><div class="flex flex-col items-stretch gap-2 p-4"><a href="https://ui.tinybird.co/login" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="inline-block border-2 text-center text-button rounded whitespace-nowrap hover:no-underline py-[6px] px-4 bg-v-bg-button text-v-text-button border-transparent hover:border-v-border-button-hover inline-flex items-center"><div class="flex gap-2 items-center justify-center"><div>Start building</div></div></a><a class="text-button text-center py-1" href="https://ui.tinybird.co/login">Sign In</a></div></div></div></nav></aside><main class="w-full grow pt-6 pb-6 md:pt-8 sm:pb-8 md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird">Deployment options</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Migrate from Classic</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="migrate-from-tinybird-classic" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Migrate from Tinybird Classic<a class="headerlink" href="#migrate-from-tinybird-classic" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>Tinybird Forward introduces a new way of working with your data projects, with changes to APIs and CLI that may be incompatible with Classic. If you&#x27;re starting a new project, see the <a href="/docs/forward">Get started</a> guide.</p><h2 id="considerations-before-migrating" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Considerations before migrating<a class="headerlink" href="#considerations-before-migrating" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Before migrating your workspace from Tinybird Classic, understand these key differences in Forward:</p><ul><li>Development happens locally using the <a href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird/local">Tinybird Local container</a>, not in the UI.</li><li>Before starting the migration, remove all the branches that are not the main one. That can be done from the UI or using <a href="/docs/classic/cli/command-ref#tb-branch">the CLI</a>.</li><li>Contact the Tinybird support team to remove any existing rollback releases. Only the live release must remain to proceed with the migration.</li><li>The Tinybird support team will need to <a href="#contact-support-to-enable-the-forward-feature-flag">enable a feature flag</a> to complete the migration to Forward.</li><li>The following features have limitations or require changes:</li></ul><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Feature</th><th>Status</th><th>Solution/Alternative</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>DynamoDB connector</td><td>Not supported</td><td>No alternative available yet. Pause migration if you depend on DynamoDB connectors.</td></tr><tr><td>BI Connector</td><td>Not supported</td><td>Use the <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/clickhouse-interface">ClickHouse HTTP Interface</a> instead. Most BI tools support ClickHouse HTTP connections.</td></tr><tr><td>Shared data sources</td><td>Partially supported</td><td>Data source sharing is <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/data-sources#share-a-data-source">supported</a>, but you cannot create Materialized Views from shared data sources in the destination workspace. Create Materialized Views in the source workspace instead.</td></tr><tr><td>Include files</td><td>Not supported</td><td>Use <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret">tb secret</a> for connector credentials and <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/pipes#create-generic-pipes">generic pipes</a> to reuse query logic. See <a href="#replace-include-files">Replace include files</a> for migration steps.</td></tr><tr><td><code>VERSION</code> tag in datafiles</td><td>Not supported</td><td>Remove any <code>VERSION</code> tags from your datafiles before migrating.</td></tr><tr><td>CI/CD workflows</td><td>Different commands</td><td>Forward uses different CLI commands. See <a href="/docs/forward/test-and-deploy/deployments/cicd">CI/CD</a> for details.</td></tr><tr><td>Testing strategy</td><td>Different approach</td><td>Regression tests and data quality tests are not supported in Forward. Fixture tests have been enhanced for easier test creation and management. See <a href="/docs/forward/test-and-deploy/test-your-project">Test your project</a> for details.</td></tr><tr><td>Resource-scoped tokens with <code>:sql_filter</code></td><td>Not supported</td><td>Remove all tokens using the <code>:sql_filter</code> suffix (e.g., <code>DATASOURCES:READ:datasource_name:sql_filter</code>) before migrating. Use <a href="/docs/forward/administration/tokens/jwt">JWTs</a> instead.</td></tr><tr><td>AWS External IDs (S3 connectors/Sinks)</td><td>Breaking change</td><td>External IDs change from workspace ID to connection name. Update AWS Trust Policies before migrating. See <a href="#external-id-changes-for-aws-integrations">External ID changes for AWS integrations</a> for details.</td></tr><tr><td><code>TYPE endpoint</code> to the .pipe files</td><td>Breaking change</td><td>Add <code>TYPE endpoint</code> parameter to the .pipe files to publish them as API endpoints</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p>If these changes work for your use case, continue reading to learn how to migrate.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-caution text-[#856100]"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0 0-3.493 0l-5.334 9.334a2 2 0 0 0 1.707 3.02h10.747a2 2 0 0 0 1.74-3.02m-1.154 1.333a.67.67 0 0 1-.586.34H2.96a.67.67 0 0 1-.587-.34.67.67 0 0 1 0-.667L7.707 2.53a.667.667 0 0 1 1.186 0l5.367 9.333a.67.67 0 0 1 .033.68zm-5.96-7.647a.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v2.667a.667.667 0 1 0 1.333 0V5.549a.667.667 0 0 0-.667-.667"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Migration is permanent and cannot be reversed. After deploying with Forward, you cannot switch your workspace back to Classic.</p></div></div><h2 id="external-id-changes-for-aws-integrations" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">External ID changes for AWS integrations<a class="headerlink" href="#external-id-changes-for-aws-integrations" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-warning text-error"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12 1.25C6.063 1.25 1.25 6.063 1.25 12S6.063 22.75 12 22.75 22.75 17.937 22.75 12 17.937 1.25 12 1.25M2.75 12A9.25 9.25 0 0 1 12 2.75c2.284 0 4.376.828 5.99 2.2l-.02.02-13 13-.02.02A9.2 9.2 0 0 1 2.75 12m3.26 7.05A9.25 9.25 0 0 0 19.05 6.01l-.019.02-13 13z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If you use AWS integrations (S3 connectors or S3 Sinks), you must update your AWS Trust Policies before migrating to Forward.</p></div></div><p>In Classic, Tinybird uses the workspace ID as the seed for generating External IDs, while in Forward it uses the connection name. This means the same connection will have a different External ID after migration.</p><h3 id="update-aws-trust-policy" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Update AWS Trust Policy<a class="headerlink" href="#update-aws-trust-policy" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>To get the new External ID for your connection, access:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">https://&lt;your_host&gt;/v0/integrations/s3/policies/trust-policy \
  ?external_id_seed={CONNECTION_NAME} \ # Replace with your connection name
  &amp;token={YOUR_ADMIN_TOKEN} # Replace with your admin token
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This returns a Trust Policy with the new External ID. Add this new External ID to your existing Trust Policy&#x27;s <code>sts:ExternalId</code> array to maintain access during and after migration.</p><h3 id="additional-s3-sinks-permission" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Additional S3 Sinks permission<a class="headerlink" href="#additional-s3-sinks-permission" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>If you use S3 Sinks, add the <code>s3:GetBucketLocation</code> permission to your AWS Access Policy. This requirement allows connections to work with buckets across multiple regions without specifying the region when creating the connection, making it more flexible for multi-region deployments.</p><h2 id="migrate-your-workspace" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Migrate your workspace<a class="headerlink" href="#migrate-your-workspace" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="steps-container"><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">1</div><div class="content"><h3 id="install-the-tinybird-forward-cli" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Install the Tinybird Forward CLI<a class="headerlink" href="#install-the-tinybird-forward-cli" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Run the following command to install the Tinybird Forward CLI and the Tinybird Local container:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><article><div class="w-full"><div class="bg-bg-darkest rounded-t-md overflow-hidden"><ul role="tablist" class="relative flex justify-start list-none ps-0 before:h-2 before:bg-bg-darkest before:w-full before:absolute before:-bottom-1 before:-z-[1]"><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all bg-bg-dark font-bold">For macOS and Linux</button></li><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all opacity-60 hover:opacity-100 hover:underline hover:font-bold">For Windows</button></li></ul></div><div class="code-tab-content [&amp;_.snippet]:rounded-t-none"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">curl https://tinybird.co | sh
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div></article></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>See <a href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird">install Tinybird Forward</a> for more information.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-caution text-[#856100]"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0 0-3.493 0l-5.334 9.334a2 2 0 0 0 1.707 3.02h10.747a2 2 0 0 0 1.74-3.02m-1.154 1.333a.67.67 0 0 1-.586.34H2.96a.67.67 0 0 1-.587-.34.67.67 0 0 1 0-.667L7.707 2.53a.667.667 0 0 1 1.186 0l5.367 9.333a.67.67 0 0 1 .033.68zm-5.96-7.647a.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v2.667a.667.667 0 1 0 1.333 0V5.549a.667.667 0 0 0-.667-.667"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>Managing CLI Versions</strong>: Having both Tinybird Classic and Forward CLIs installed can cause version conflicts since both use the <code>tb</code> command. To avoid these conflicts, consider:</p><ol><li>Using the uv Python package manager to keep both CLIs completely isolated (recommended):</li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default"># For Classic CLI
uvx --from tinybird-cli@latest tb

# For Forward CLI
uvx --from tinybird@latest tb
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><ol start="2"><li>Creating aliases in your shell configuration:</li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default"># Add to .bashrc or .zshrc
alias tb-classic=&quot;path/to/classic/tb&quot;
alias tb-forward=&quot;path/to/forward/tb&quot;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><ol start="3"><li>Using separate virtual environments for each CLI version.</li></ol><p>This ensures you use the correct CLI version for each operation during migration.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>The following steps use the uv Python package.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">2</div><div class="content"><h3 id="authenticate-to-your-workspace" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Authenticate to your workspace<a class="headerlink" href="#authenticate-to-your-workspace" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Authenticate to your workspace using the Classic CLI:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird-cli@latest tb auth --interactive
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Follow the prompts to complete authentication.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">3</div><div class="content"><h3 id="pull-your-project" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Pull your project<a class="headerlink" href="#pull-your-project" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>If you already have the latest version of your datafiles locally (e.g. from your Git repo), skip to the next step.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>If you don&#x27;t have your datafiles locally, pull them from Tinybird using the Forward CLI:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud pull
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">4</div><div class="content"><h3 id="check-deployment-compatibility" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Check deployment compatibility<a class="headerlink" href="#check-deployment-compatibility" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Validate your project&#x27;s compatibility with the Forward CLI:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud deploy --check
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>You should see:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">* No changes to be deployed
* No changes in tokens to be deployed
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>If you encounter any errors, it&#x27;s recommended to fix them in your Classic workspace so you can have a &quot;clean&quot; first Forward deployment. See <a href="#common-migration-errors">common migration errors</a> for information about common errors and fixes.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Fix all of the errors, repull your workspace (if necessary), and rerun the deployment check until there are no changes detected.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">5</div><div class="content"><h3 id="contact-support-to-enable-the-forward-feature-flag" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Contact support to enable the Forward feature flag<a class="headerlink" href="#contact-support-to-enable-the-forward-feature-flag" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Once your project passes the compatibility check, contact Tinybird support (<a href="mailto:support@tinybird.co" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="inline-flex items-center">support@tinybird.co</a>) to enable the Forward feature flag for your workspace.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">6</div><div class="content"><h3 id="trigger-a-deployment" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Trigger a deployment<a class="headerlink" href="#trigger-a-deployment" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Once the feature flag is enabled, it&#x27;s time to trigger a deployment.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>To create a simple first deployment, generate a dummy endpoint as the only change:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="forward_dummy_endpoint.pipe">forward_dummy_endpoint.pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">NODE n
SQL &gt;
    SELECT &#x27;forward&#x27;

TYPE endpoint
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>There are two ways to <a href="/docs/forward/test-and-deploy/deployments">deploy your project</a>:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h4 id="option-1-cicd-recommended" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Option 1: CI/CD (recommended)<a class="headerlink" href="#option-1-cicd-recommended" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>In an empty directory outside of your existing project, generate default CI/CD workflows by running the following command:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird@latest tb init --type cli --dev-mode manual --folder .
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p><code>tb init</code> creates the scaffolding for a new project. Use <code>--cicd github</code> or <code>--cicd gitlab</code> to generate CI/CD templates. Review the workflows, edit them as desired, and add the files to the root of your project.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Finally, trigger the deployment by committing your project to Git and creating a merge/pull request.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h4 id="option-2-cli" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Option 2: CLI<a class="headerlink" href="#option-2-cli" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>If you don&#x27;t have CI/CD configured, you can deploy manually:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud deploy
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">7</div><div class="content"><h3 id="open-the-project-in-tinybird-cloud" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Open the project in Tinybird Cloud<a class="headerlink" href="#open-the-project-in-tinybird-cloud" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>After the deployment succeeds, open the project in Tinybird Cloud by running the following command:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">uvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud open
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div></div><p>The migration is complete! Your project will continue working as expected; you do not need to change your tokens, endpoint URLs, or anything else.</p><h2 id="common-migration-errors" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Common migration errors<a class="headerlink" href="#common-migration-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Common errors and changes include (but are not limited to):</p><h3 id="missing-connection-files" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Missing connection files<a class="headerlink" href="#missing-connection-files" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>In Forward, <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/connection-files">.connection files</a> are used to store your connector details.</p><p>You need to create .connection files to enable your connections to Kafka, S3, or GCS. If you manually pulled your datafiles, the .connection files were created, but they are empty.</p><p>See <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors">Connectors</a> for more information about the syntax.</p><h3 id="kafka-settings-have-been-deprecated" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Kafka settings have been deprecated<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-settings-have-been-deprecated" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Some settings in the Kafka connector have been deprecated. You need to update your Kafka .connection file to use the most up-to-date <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka#kafka-connection-settings">Kafka settings</a>.</p><h3 id="replace-include-files" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Replace include files<a class="headerlink" href="#replace-include-files" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Include files are not supported in Forward. The fix depends on your use of include files:</p><ul><li>If you use include files to store secrets, use <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret">tb secret</a> to set secrets in your local and cloud environments.</li><li>If you use include files to reuse query logic, you can create <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/pipes#create-generic-pipes">generic pipes</a> and reference them in your endpoint pipes. For example:</li></ul><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="reusable_filters.pipe">reusable_filters.pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">NODE apply_params
SQL &gt;
    %
    SELECT * FROM my_datasource
    WHERE
        tenant_id = {{ String(tenant) }}
        AND date BETWEEN {{ Date(start_date) }} AND {{ Date(end_date) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="my_endpoint.pipe">my_endpoint.pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">NODE endpoint
SQL &gt;
    %
    SELECT * FROM reusable_filters

TYPE endpoint
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="add-type-endpoint-to-your-pipe-files" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Add TYPE endpoint to your .pipe files<a class="headerlink" href="#add-type-endpoint-to-your-pipe-files" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>You need to add <code>TYPE endpoint</code> to your .pipe files so they can be published as API endpoints.</p><p>If you omit the <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/pipe-files#available-instructions"><code>TYPE</code> instruction</a>, the pipe will be a generic pipe that is not publicly exposed.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="example.pipe">example.pipe</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">NODE my_node
SQL &gt;
    SELECT * FROM my_datasource

TYPE endpoint
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="next-steps" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Next steps<a class="headerlink" href="#next-steps" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ul><li>Learn about working with Forward in the <a href="/docs/forward">Forward documentation</a>.</li></ul></article><div Migrate from Tinybird Classic\nmeta:\n    description: Migrate your project from Tinybird Classic to Tinybird Forward.\n---\n\n# Migrate from Tinybird Classic\n\nTinybird Forward introduces a new way of working with your data projects, with changes to APIs and CLI that may be incompatible with Classic. If you're starting a new project, see the [Get started](/forward) guide.\n\n## Considerations before migrating\n\nBefore migrating your workspace from Tinybird Classic, understand these key differences in Forward:\n\n- Development happens locally using the [Tinybird Local container](/forward/install-tinybird/local), not in the UI.\n- Before starting the migration, remove all the branches that are not the main one. That can be done from the UI or using [the CLI](/classic/cli/command-ref#tb-branch).\n- Contact the Tinybird support team to remove any existing rollback releases. Only the live release must remain to proceed with the migration.\n- The Tinybird support team will need to [enable a feature flag](#contact-support-to-enable-the-forward-feature-flag) to complete the migration to Forward.\n- The following features have limitations or require changes:\n\n{% table %}\n  * Feature\n  * Status\n  * Solution/Alternative\n  ---\n  * DynamoDB connector\n  * Not supported\n  * No alternative available yet. Pause migration if you depend on DynamoDB connectors.\n  ---\n  * BI Connector\n  * Not supported\n  * Use the [ClickHouse HTTP Interface](/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/clickhouse-interface) instead. Most BI tools support ClickHouse HTTP connections.\n  ---\n  * Shared data sources\n  * Partially supported\n  * Data source sharing is [supported](/forward/get-data-in/data-sources#share-a-data-source), but you cannot create Materialized Views from shared data sources in the destination workspace. Create Materialized Views in the source workspace instead.\n  ---\n  * Include files\n  * Not supported\n  * Use [tb secret](/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret) for connector credentials and [generic pipes](/forward/work-with-data/pipes#create-generic-pipes) to reuse query logic. See [Replace include files](#replace-include-files) for migration steps.\n  ---\n  * `VERSION` tag in datafiles\n  * Not supported\n  * Remove any `VERSION` tags from your datafiles before migrating.\n  ---\n  * CI/CD workflows\n  * Different commands\n  * Forward uses different CLI commands. See [CI/CD](/forward/test-and-deploy/deployments/cicd) for details.\n  ---\n  * Testing strategy\n  * Different approach\n  * Regression tests and data quality tests are not supported in Forward. Fixture tests have been enhanced for easier test creation and management. See [Test your project](/forward/test-and-deploy/test-your-project) for details.\n  ---\n  * Resource-scoped tokens with `:sql_filter`\n  * Not supported\n  * Remove all tokens using the `:sql_filter` suffix (e.g., `DATASOURCES:READ:datasource_name:sql_filter`) before migrating. Use [JWTs](/forward/administration/tokens/jwt) instead.\n  ---\n  * AWS External IDs (S3 connectors/Sinks)\n  * Breaking change\n  * External IDs change from workspace ID to connection name. Update AWS Trust Policies before migrating. See [External ID changes for AWS integrations](#external-id-changes-for-aws-integrations) for details.\n  ---\n  * `TYPE endpoint` to the .pipe files\n  * Breaking change\n  * Add `TYPE endpoint` parameter to the .pipe files to publish them as API endpoints\n{% /table %}\n\nIf these changes work for your use case, continue reading to learn how to migrate.\n\n{% callout type=\"caution\" %}\nMigration is permanent and cannot be reversed. After deploying with Forward, you cannot switch your workspace back to Classic.\n{% /callout %}\n\n## External ID changes for AWS integrations\n\n{% callout type=\"warning\" %}\nIf you use AWS integrations (S3 connectors or S3 Sinks), you must update your AWS Trust Policies before migrating to Forward.\n{% /callout %}\n\nIn Classic, Tinybird uses the workspace ID as the seed for generating External IDs, while in Forward it uses the connection name. This means the same connection will have a different External ID after migration.\n\n### Update AWS Trust Policy\n\nTo get the new External ID for your connection, access:\n\n```shell\n{% user(\"apiHost\") %}/v0/integrations/s3/policies/trust-policy \\\n  ?external_id_seed={CONNECTION_NAME} \\ # Replace with your connection name\n  \u0026token={YOUR_ADMIN_TOKEN} # Replace with your admin token\n```\n\nThis returns a Trust Policy with the new External ID. Add this new External ID to your existing Trust Policy's `sts:ExternalId` array to maintain access during and after migration.\n\n### Additional S3 Sinks permission\n\nIf you use S3 Sinks, add the `s3:GetBucketLocation` permission to your AWS Access Policy. This requirement allows connections to work with buckets across multiple regions without specifying the region when creating the connection, making it more flexible for multi-region deployments.\n\n## Migrate your workspace\n\n{% steps %}\n\n### Install the Tinybird Forward CLI\n\nRun the following command to install the Tinybird Forward CLI and the Tinybird Local container:\n\n{% snippet title=\"install-tinybird-forward\" /%}\n\nSee [install Tinybird Forward](/forward/install-tinybird) for more information.\n\n{% callout type=\"caution\" %}\n**Managing CLI Versions**: Having both Tinybird Classic and Forward CLIs installed can cause version conflicts since both use the `tb` command. To avoid these conflicts, consider:\n\n1. Using the uv Python package manager to keep both CLIs completely isolated (recommended):\n\n```bash\n# For Classic CLI\nuvx --from tinybird-cli@latest tb\n\n# For Forward CLI\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb\n```\n\n2. Creating aliases in your shell configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Add to .bashrc or .zshrc\nalias tb-classic=\"path/to/classic/tb\"\nalias tb-forward=\"path/to/forward/tb\"\n```\n\n3. Using separate virtual environments for each CLI version.\n\nThis ensures you use the correct CLI version for each operation during migration.\n{% /callout %}\n\nThe following steps use the uv Python package.\n\n### Authenticate to your workspace\n\nAuthenticate to your workspace using the Classic CLI:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird-cli@latest tb auth --interactive\n```\n\nFollow the prompts to complete authentication.\n\n### Pull your project\n\nIf you already have the latest version of your datafiles locally (e.g. from your Git repo), skip to the next step.\n\nIf you don't have your datafiles locally, pull them from Tinybird using the Forward CLI:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud pull\n```\n\n### Check deployment compatibility\n\nValidate your project's compatibility with the Forward CLI:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud deploy --check\n```\n\nYou should see:\n```bash\n* No changes to be deployed\n* No changes in tokens to be deployed\n```\n\nIf you encounter any errors, it's recommended to fix them in your Classic workspace so you can have a \"clean\" first Forward deployment. See [common migration errors](#common-migration-errors) for information about common errors and fixes.\n\nFix all of the errors, repull your workspace (if necessary), and rerun the deployment check until there are no changes detected.\n\n### Contact support to enable the Forward feature flag\n\nOnce your project passes the compatibility check, contact Tinybird support (\u003csupport@tinybird.co\u003e) to enable the Forward feature flag for your workspace.\n\n### Trigger a deployment\n\nOnce the feature flag is enabled, it's time to trigger a deployment.\n\nTo create a simple first deployment, generate a dummy endpoint as the only change:\n\n```tb {% title=\"forward_dummy_endpoint.pipe\" %}\nNODE n\nSQL \u003e\n    SELECT 'forward'\n\nTYPE endpoint\n```\n\nThere are two ways to [deploy your project](/forward/test-and-deploy/deployments):\n\n#### Option 1: CI/CD (recommended)\n\nIn an empty directory outside of your existing project, generate default CI/CD workflows by running the following command:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb init --type cli --dev-mode manual --folder .\n```\n\n`tb init` creates the scaffolding for a new project. Use `--cicd github` or `--cicd gitlab` to generate CI/CD templates. Review the workflows, edit them as desired, and add the files to the root of your project.\n\nFinally, trigger the deployment by committing your project to Git and creating a merge/pull request.\n\n#### Option 2: CLI\n\nIf you don't have CI/CD configured, you can deploy manually:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud deploy\n```\n\n### Open the project in Tinybird Cloud\n\nAfter the deployment succeeds, open the project in Tinybird Cloud by running the following command:\n\n```bash\nuvx --from tinybird@latest tb --cloud open\n```\n\n{% /steps %}\n\nThe migration is complete! Your project will continue working as expected; you do not need to change your tokens, endpoint URLs, or anything else.\n\n## Common migration errors\n\nCommon errors and changes include (but are not limited to):\n\n### Missing connection files\n\nIn Forward, [.connection files](/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/connection-files) are used to store your connector details.\n\nYou need to create .connection files to enable your connections to Kafka, S3, or GCS. If you manually pulled your datafiles, the .connection files were created, but they are empty.\n\n See [Connectors](/forward/get-data-in/connectors) for more information about the syntax.\n\n### Kafka settings have been deprecated\n\nSome settings in the Kafka connector have been deprecated. You need to update your Kafka .connection file to use the most up-to-date [Kafka settings](/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka#kafka-connection-settings).\n\n\n### Replace include files\n\nInclude files are not supported in Forward. The fix depends on your use of include files:\n\n- If you use include files to store secrets, use [tb secret](/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret) to set secrets in your local and cloud environments.\n- If you use include files to reuse query logic, you can create [generic pipes](/forward/work-with-data/pipes#create-generic-pipes) and reference them in your endpoint pipes. For example:\n\n```tb {% title=\"reusable_filters.pipe\" %}\nNODE apply_params\nSQL \u003e\n    %\n    SELECT * FROM my_datasource\n    WHERE\n        tenant_id = {{ String(tenant) }}\n        AND date BETWEEN {{ Date(start_date) }} AND {{ Date(end_date) }}\n```\n\n```tb {% title=\"my_endpoint.pipe\" %}\nNODE endpoint\nSQL \u003e\n    %\n    SELECT * FROM reusable_filters\n\nTYPE endpoint\n```\n\n### Add TYPE endpoint to your .pipe files\n\nYou need to add `TYPE endpoint` to your .pipe files so they can be published as API endpoints.\n\nIf you omit the [`TYPE` instruction](/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/pipe-files#available-instructions), the pipe will be a generic pipe that is not publicly exposed.\n\n```tb {% title=\"example.pipe\" %}\nNODE my_node\nSQL \u003e\n    SELECT * FROM my_datasource\n\nTYPE endpoint\n```\n\n## Next steps\n\n* Learn about working with Forward in the [Forward documentation](/forward).\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"2a:{\"fill\":\"currentColor\",\"d\":\"M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0
